Activated the **second dormant column, `gym_profiles.disputed_items`** (D-60 §5 deferred the curator-review mechanism as TBD §10; this builds it). **Capture** (`routes/locales._edit_locale` inherit branch → new `_record_profile_edit`; `templates/locales/form.html` inherit-mode checkbox): a peer's shared-vs-submitted delta is recorded as a correction proposal **only when they tick the explicit "the shared profile is wrong" box** (keeps personal overrides out of the queue — Andy 2026-06-29) — JSON `[{by, adds, removes, at}]`, one open per (profile, peer); an unflagged save or a matching view withdraws; invalid tags dropped; the box is pre-checked when a proposal is already pending. **Review** (`routes/admin.py` `/admin/gym-profile-edits` + `templates/admin/gym_profile_edits.html`): `_list_pending_profile_edits` lists non-private profiles with proposals; `_review_profile_edit` approve folds adds/removes into the shared `equipment` (every inheritor picks it up via the **existing** `_shared_equipment_set`) + advances `last_confirmed_by`, reject drops it; audited like `resolve_flag`. Dashboard nav link added. **No plan-gen/Layer-2C change** (the "disputed ⇒ not-available" treatment is deferred). Tests: `test_locales` +10, `test_redesign_admin_render` +2; full suite 3773 passed/30 skipped.
- **Slice 1 shipped (PR [#1009](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/1009), branch `claude/issue-971-hmi0ro`; handoff `…CrowdSourcedGymHotelProfiles_971_Slice1_NameGeoDedup_2026_06_29…`):** activated the dormant `gym_profiles.address_fingerprint` column. `routes/locales._address_fingerprint(name, lat, lng)` = lowercased+punct-collapsed name + coords on a ~111 m grid (`name|lat.3f|lng.3f`; `None` when name/coords missing); `_find_gym_profile_by_fingerprint` is the mapbox-miss fallback (excludes `private` per #446); `_create_gym_profile` stamps it (appended LAST in the INSERT so `private` stays param idx 6); `_resolve_shared_profile` falls back to it only when the `mapbox_id` lookup misses.

A future fingerprint backfill would need a join `gym_profiles ← locale_profiles.gym_profile_id` for coords (deferred). (Slice 3) B inherits A's shared profile, saves a changed equipment view → proposal appears at `/admin/gym-profile-edits`; admin **approve** updates the shared profile (A + all inheritors see it), **reject** leaves it; B re-saving a matching view withdraws the proposal.

## Layer 3 / process — Slice 3 gating + collision + CI quirk (2026-06-22)

- **Parallel-build collision (lesson).** #865 (a session branch) and #868 (another session) both built #214/#213 Slice 2; #868 merged first, #865 closed as superseded. The duplicate was invisible until `git fetch origin main` during rebase. **When running concurrent Claude sessions on one epic, at session start `git fetch origin main` + check the issue (e.g. #213/#214) for an existing PR/branch/merged commit before building.** Rule #9 extended to the remote.
- **CI-trigger quirk.** Commits pushed from a Claude session branch (container git path) may **not** trigger the `CI` workflow (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`), even though the commit reaches GitHub and Vercel builds it (Vercel uses its own webhook). Symptom: PR head shows only the `Vercel` status; `actions_list` shows zero CI runs for the branch while other `claude/*` PRs trigger fine. **Workaround:** `actions_run_trigger run_workflow` (`workflow_dispatch`) on `ci.yml` against the branch — its jobs post the required check contexts on the head commit by name, satisfying branch protection; auto-merge then fires. (Confirmed 2026-06-22, run #763.)
- **Layer 3D #213 staleness re-fire SHIPPED as #880's Reading-B; #881 Reading-A consolidated out (2026-06-22).** **Parallel-build collision:** #881 (this branch) built the staleness fingerprint as **Reading-A** (`evaluated_against` = *computed* 2A/2C/2D payload hashes, `compute_gate_fingerprint`); #880 (`claude/serene-newton-igye62`, `5959ed7`) shipped the same #213 staleness as **Reading-B** — `input_fingerprint` = a SHA-256 over the **raw leaf inputs** (`compute_gate_input_fingerprint`, no LLM) **plus the on-view consumer** (`routes/plan_create.py` re-entry/acknowledge/generate → re-kick the row to `generating` = the async recompute via the poller). Both merged (disjoint lines, never CI'd together) → main briefly carried both, mine dead (unread) + polluting `evaluated_against`. **Andy: consolidate on Reading-B** (cheaper — no cone rebuild; already ships the consumer). Cleanup PR reverts #881's Reading-A code + rewrites `Layer3D_Spec` §6.1/§6.1.1/§11.2 to Reading-B; `evaluated_against` restored to the etl-provenance stamp. Combined main green (128 gate+#880 tests). The earlier **#874** (`stale: bool` + sync re-gate) was closed superseded before all this. **Review-screen UX remainder SHIPPED (2026-06-22, branch `claude/brave-rubin-ikblc4`):** (1) `[Fix this]` revise links (`plan_create._build_revise_urls` → `profile.injuries`=`injuries.list_entries`, `profile.disciplines`/`.nutrition`/`.availability`=**`profile.edit`** [Rule #9: NOT `locales.edit_profile` — that's the per-locale *equipment* editor; the three live on the athlete profile page], `h2.*`=**`race_events.edit_race`** [not the handoff's `race_event_edit`]; fail-safe, falls back to the text stub for unmapped `h3.*` / unresolvable surfaces); (2) 3A/3B prompt-rev pointer comments (bump `LAYER3_GATE_PROMPT_REVISION`); (3) `_rekick_stale_gate` Rule #15 telemetry print. The #874 `5b4de06` form/`_REVISE_TARGET_ENDPOINTS` reuse was moot — `5b4de06` is gone from the remote (closed branch), and #880's fingerprint auto-detects staleness on re-entry so a plain link suffices (no `revised`-resolution form needed). **Still owed: only live-verify (Andy)** — park a plan → each item links to the right editor; edit a field, re-enter `/review` → re-kicks + re-evaluates; `/admin/logs` shows `_rekick_stale_gate:`. Then **3C** (#844) is all that's left on the 3D node. Handoffs `…Slice3a_Fingerprint…` (§9 = consolidation) + `…Layer3D_ReviseLinks_213…` (this slice).
- **Test-run gotcha + fix (container, 2026-06-22).** Route modules (`routes.plan_create`, …) open a Neon connect **at import time**, which **hangs** in the container (Neon egress blocked) — so any test importing the Flask app (e.g. `tests/test_layer3d_wiring.py`) hangs on collection. **Fix (from #880's handoff, verified this session — 62 passed incl. the wiring suite):** point `DATABASE_URL` at a dead localhost so the import-time connect *fast-fails* instead of hanging — `DATABASE_URL="postgresql://u:p@127.0.0.1:5999/none?connect_timeout=2" /tmp/venv/bin/python -m pytest tests/test_layer3d_wiring.py tests/test_layer3d_gate.py -q` — run with `dangerouslyDisableSandbox: true` + a `timeout` (else the harness sandbox terminates any pytest that touches network mid-collection: silent 0-byte output, exit 1). App-free files (e.g. `tests/test_layer3d_gate.py`) run without the shim; front-load a `tests/test_layer4_*.py` to dodge the isolated-single-file circular-import quirk.
- **3C SHIPPED + surfacing story complete (2026-06-23).** The line above ("3C is all that's left on the 3D node") is now closed: 3C built as #844/#911 (CN-1/CN-2 + `surface_orphaned_flags`), then **Item B** (green-plan coaching notes) shipped on `claude/awesome-ride-5j0m3k` (`f6deab7`, PR-pending) — informational gate items now list on the plan home (`view_plan` → `view.html` via `_plan_coaching_notes`), closing the gap where a green plan hid its surfaced flags. **Remaining 3C levers (none buildable now, per the kickoff §2 map `…Layer3C_ConflictDetection_NextSteps…`):** Item A flag→`warning` promotions are **prod-signal-gated** (flip a §7.1 ★ into `_FLAG_WARNING` only on a real informational miss); Item C CN-3+ new detectors are **STOP-AND-ASK** (Trigger #5 + spec-first; don't build speculatively). **Owed live-verifies (Andy):** the #213 revise-links/staleness walk (above, still open) + the optional Item-B visual check (a green plan with ≥1 informational flag shows the Coaching-notes panel — render-test-covered). 3C may be done for v1.

## Provider integrations & API — ACTIVE THREAD (next focus, Andy 2026-06-20)

The #767 manual file-upload sub-track is **COMPLETE** (slices 1+2+4 merged, 3 retired, **5 merged `#785`**, **#767 CLOSED**) — any device that *exports a file* (`.fit/.tcx/.gpx/.csv`, incl. zips) ingests via the one auto-detecting uploader on the Data hub. But "integration/API work" as a whole is **not** done. Three open work-streams, in rough build order:

## #803 StrengthExercise resolution-tier crash — deterministic fix, all 4 synth paths (2026-06-20; PR [#807](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/807), auto-merge armed) — pushed; plan-regen live-verify owed
- **Root cause:** the synthesizer emitted **tier-1 (exact)** `StrengthExercise` picks that *also* carried a `substitute_text` → the `StrengthExercise` tier↔field validator (`payload._check_resolution_tier`) raised → the Build block fumbled (no retry budget on the long block call) → the whole plan failed (pv76/pv77). It's a cross-field rule the JSON tool schema can't express + the prompt only half-stated. **#777 exposed it** (MTB/packraft strength pool 0→37 turned the substitution path ON).
- **Fix (option C — deterministic, Andy-ratified):** `per_phase._apply_strength_resolution(raw_sessions, layer2c_payloads)` + `_strength_resolution_fields(rx)` overwrite `resolution_tier`/`substitute_text`/`proxy_origin_id` from each pick's **enum-locked `exercise_id` → 2C resolution at the session's locale**, *before* `StrengthExercise(**e)`. Wired at **all four** construction sites (`per_phase` / `single_session` [locale-gated] / `plan_refresh` / `race_week_brief`). Helpers in `per_phase`; siblings already import it (no new cycle). `per_phase.SYSTEM_PROMPT` strength bullet rewritten (system derives the tier) + `LAYER4_PROMPT_REVISION 18→19`. Strict `model_validator` kept as backstop. No schema/contract/migration change. **3001 passed / 30 skipped.**
- **LIVE-VERIFY owed (Andy-action — container can't run plan-gen):** regenerate the MTB+packraft PGE plan → reaches `ready`, no `StrengthExercise` `ValidationError` in `/admin/logs`. **Folds into the Plan-75 regen below** (same arc — #777 turned on the path #803 fixes).
- **Carried, separate (NOT fixed — Rule #16):** an over-budget attempt-1 that parse-fails gets no retry, so one bad block call still fumbles the plan. #803 removes the *most-likely* parse failure; the no-retry-on-overbudget structural issue is its own follow-up if it recurs.

## FIT-import prod incident + hub uploader unify (2026-06-19) — FIXED; one residual (#747)
- **`init_postgres` silently aborted on every cold start since #733 (2026-06-18).** A `;` inside a SQL comment in `PG_SCHEMA` broke the char-based `PG_SCHEMA.split(';')` into a bare-text fragment that syntax-errored in the UNGUARDED schema loop (caught only by app.py's broad `except` → "DB init skipped"). Net: **no schema/migration from #733 on reached prod** — `provider_value_map`, `provider_raw_record` (Slice 1), `cardio_log.discipline_id` (Slice 2a) all absent until **PR #742** (remove the `;` + per-statement-guard the schema loop + Rule #15 log + `tests/test_init_db_schema.py`). Surfaced as a prod `500 UndefinedColumn discipline_id` on a real FIT import. **Verified fixed via `neon-query`:** provider_value_map (263 rows) + provider_raw_record + discipline_id now live.
- **§5 Slice-2 live-verify (MTB) — DONE:** re-import landed `cardio_log` row `Mountain Biking, discipline_id=D-008`. Trail-run → D-001 half still optional (not required).
- **RESIDUAL — issue [#747](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/747) (low-pri hardening):** (1) `PG_SCHEMA.split(';')` is char-based — any `;` in a string literal / CHECK / comment re-breaks it (the regression test guards comments only; the splitter is the real fragility); (2) the seed steps AFTER the migration loop in `init_postgres` are still unguarded. Acute bug fixed + regression-tested; this is "don't let the class recur structurally."
- **Hub FIT uploader unified (PRs #744 / #746):** the Connections-hub drop card was a fake single-file form → now the real multi-file bulk uploader (`data-bulk-*`), and `import_bulk` routes **both** workout + wellness FITs by FileId kind via a shared `_ingest_wellness_fit` helper. A window-level file-drop guard in `app.js` keeps a stray drop from navigating the browser to the file. The dedicated `/import-wellness` page is untouched.
- **Standing lesson (Rule #9/#10 gap):** a green `verify-handoff.sh` + clean on-disk anchors do **not** prove prod applied a migration. The container can't reach Neon, so for any "schema/migration is live" claim, a read-only `neon-query` is the only proof of the DB half.

- **MERGED (PR #723, 2026-06-18, squash).** `specs/Provider_Inbound_Matrix_v2.md` (v1 superseded → `archive/superseded-specs/`). ## Ops automation / operating model — LIVE (2026-06-15; record issue #630)

**This changed how we work. Read it before doing prod DB ops or merges.** The web container can't reach Neon, but GitHub Actions can — so prod DB work + merges run in the cloud, Claude drives them, and Andy only approves the irreversible bits ("decide-not-do"; Andy is mobile / device-changing, consistent access = Claude Code web/Android). All of the below is built, merged, and **test-fired green** this session.

**Operating flow (default for every change):** Claude opens a PR → `enable_pr_auto_merge` (**MERGE** — real merge commit, Andy 2026-06-29; not squash) → it **self-merges once required checks pass**. Branch protection on `main`: required checks (`Python unit suite (stubbed)` / `JS harness (jsdom)` / `Layer 0 integrity gate`), **0 approvals** (solo can't self-approve — do NOT require reviews or it deadlocks), **admin-bypass off**. Auto-merge is enabled repo-wide. Don't merge mid-run; let it land. `.github/CODEOWNERS` auto-requests Andy's review on `etl/migrations/` (soft nudge only — never flip on "require code-owner review").

> **GOTCHA — MCP-opened PRs don't trigger `ci.yml` (found 2026-06-29, #884 PR-3).** A PR opened via the GitHub MCP `create_pull_request` tool does **not** fire the `on: pull_request` workflow (GitHub suppresses workflow runs from that token to prevent recursion), so the three required checks never register and the PR can't satisfy branch protection — it strands with "Expected — waiting for status." (This stranded #990.) **Fix:** after opening such a PR, trigger CI explicitly — `actions_run_trigger run_workflow` on **`ci.yml` with `ref=<branch>`**. All three required jobs run under `workflow_dispatch` (`if: github.event_name != 'schedule'`), attach as check runs on the PR head SHA, and release auto-merge. (Pushing to the feature branch does NOT help — `ci.yml`'s `push` trigger is `branches:[main]` only.)

**Triggerable workflows** (Claude via `actions_run_trigger run_workflow`, or Andy via Actions tab → Run workflow):
- **`layer0-apply.yml`** — applies `etl/migrations/layer0/*.sql` to prod Neon, **gated by the `production` GitHub Environment** (required reviewer = Andy → one tap to approve; admin-bypass off; prevent-self-review off so Andy can approve Claude-triggered runs). Idempotent → safe to re-run. **This replaces the old "Andy pastes SQL into the Neon editor" step.**
- **`layer0-redump.yml`** (input `version`, default next) — `pg_dump`s live `layer0` → `etl/output/layer0_etl_v<ver>.sql` on branch `claude/layer0-baseline-v<ver>`; then open the PR so the `layer0-gate` validates the snapshot before merge. Keeps the committed baseline in lockstep with live (prevents the drift that caused #616).
- **`neon-query.yml`** (input `query`) — read-only diagnostic SELECT vs prod via the read-only role; read-only enforced by role grants + `default_transaction_read_only=on`; result in the job log (Claude reads via `get_job_logs`).
- **`layer0-validate-live.yml`** — **nightly** (cron `0 7 * * *`) + manual `validate_layer0` vs **live** prod via the read-only role; catches live integrity drift (the #616 `primary_movement`-clobber class) automatically + emails Andy on failure. First run PASS.

**Secrets / gates (one-time, all set):** `NEON_DATABASE_URL` (write — apply/redump) · `NEON_RO_DATABASE_URL` (read-only Neon role `claude_ro`, SELECT on `layer0`+`public` — diag/validate-live) · `production` environment (required reviewer = @ahorn885).

**Prod logs (Rule #14 — no more traceback-pasting):** `GET /admin/logs?token=<DIAG_TOKEN>` (optional `&q=<substr>&minutes=N`), fetched via the **Vercel MCP `mcp__Vercel__web_fetch_vercel_url`** tool — **NOT plain `WebFetch`**. The prod deployment is behind Vercel Authentication: an anonymous fetcher (`WebFetch`) 403s at the Vercel edge *before* the app's token gate, so a 403 there is an auth-layer block, not a bad token. The Vercel MCP tool carries the team's Vercel auth → 200 (confirmed 2026-06-16; `get_access_to_vercel_url` is the fallback for cookie-based share links). Andy pastes the current `DIAG_TOKEN` per debugging session (**chat-only, never commit**); rotated 2026-06-16 (`sk_…` form, supersedes `0dKHoR2…`). Preferred over the truncating Vercel runtime-log MCP.

**Local sync:** `.claude/settings.json` has a `SessionStart` `git pull --ff-only` hook so Andy's local clone auto-syncs with web-session merges.

## T3 plan-refresh fixes (2026-06-13, PR #569 + #572) — DONE; one live re-verify owed (post-#572)

**PR [#569](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/569) (`Closes #570`, branch `claude/plan-65-refresh-r8tclv`) squash-merged to `main`.** The live T3-refresh verify owed by the #566/#208 handoff surfaced that **T3 refresh had never worked**: `routes/plan_refresh.py` never passed `plan_start_date` to `orchestrate_plan_refresh`, so every T3 (cross-phase) refresh failed `_validate_inputs` with `plan_start_date_missing` (T1/T2 don't require it → silent). Fix: `_resolve_plan_start_date` walks `refresh_parent_version_id` to the root `plan_create` row's `scope_start_date` (the plan's true start, NOT the refresh window), threaded through `build_refresh_advance_ctx` → `run_refresh_orchestration`. **Code-only, NO DDL, nothing to deploy.** Handoff: `V5_Implementation_T3RefreshPlanStartDateFix_2026_06_13_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`.

- ✅ **#208 async/resumable refresh — confirmed live-correct.** The watch proved the plumbing: POST→302→progress→cron/poller passes, cron solo-drove after tab-close, advance-lock guard held, graceful `_mark_plan_failed` (no 504). The owed "live refresh verify" from #566 is effectively discharged for the async machinery.
- ✅ **#569 `plan_start_date` fix — CONFIRMED LIVE (2026-06-13).** The owed re-verify ran (T3 refresh of pv=65 → pv=67, `created_via=plan_refresh_t3`); pv=67 **cleared `_validate_inputs`** — no `plan_start_date_missing`. T3 refresh now reaches real synthesis.
- ✅ **NEW bug the re-verify caught + fixed: T3 synthesis output-token truncation — DONE (PR [#572](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/572), branch `claude/adoring-mccarthy-su0igw`, squash-merged to `main`).** pv=67 then hit `schema_violation … stop_reason=max_tokens, last_attempt_output_tokens=10000/ceiling=10000` — the flat 10000 output budget couldn't fit up to 56 sessions in one `record_refresh_sessions` call, so it stayed `generating` and the cron deterministically re-drove it (never `ready`). **Fix (reuse the create-path balancing, Andy's call):** new `per_phase.block_output_budget(max_sessions, floor)` = `sessions × 1400 + 2000`, clamped to `_MODEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS=64000` (Sonnet 4.6 ceiling); the refresh driver sizes `effective_max_tokens` per `_TIER_MAX_SESSIONS` (T1 7,600 / T2 21,600 / **T3 → 64,000**); T3 `DEFAULT_EXTENDED_THINKING_BUDGET` 6500→0 (so the 64K output budget doesn't push the request past the model ceiling). Create's per-phase block-mode now calls the same helper (behavior-preserving — its blocks are ≤21,600). +4 tests; full suite 2366; CI green. **Code-only, NO DDL.** Handoff: `V5_Implementation_T3RefreshOutputBudgetTruncationFix_2026_06_13_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`.
- ⬜ **OWED — Andy's-hands live T3 re-verify (post-#572 deploy).** Re-run a **T3** refresh on prod → confirm the new pv reaches `generation_status=ready` with a phase-correct `total_sessions`. Read via the diag token: Vercel MCP `web_fetch_vercel_url("…/admin/plan/<id>/diag?token=<DIAG_TOKEN>")` (direct container curl is egress-blocked; the runtime-log MCP misses `print()` failures — they log as `info`). #572 resolves realistic ~20–35-session 4-week windows (≈28–49k output, under 64K).
- 🅾️ **Optional / contingent follow-ups (build only if the trigger fires; `status:deferred`/`priority:low`):**
  - **[#574](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/574)** — decompose T3 refresh into per-week blocks (the create-path D-77 machinery NOT ported; refresh is single-call Pattern B). Trigger: a dense ≥~46-session 4-week window truncates at the 64K clamp post-#572.
  - **[#575](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/575)** — per-pass give-up backstop so a deterministic *retryable* refresh failure stops the cron re-driving it (the reason pv=67 cron-looped; create has `_PER_BLOCK_BUDGET_MS`, refresh doesn't). Adjacent to #539. Trigger: any retryable refresh failure recurs cron-looping post-#572.

## #540 Layer 4 feasibility cascade — CREATE-PATH COMPLETE (terrain #553/#556 + craft #562); refresh tail + column lift gated

**Go-live blocker #540** (sessions prescribed at locales lacking the required terrain — pv=65 Rock-Climbing-at-home). Design fully ratified with Andy (slice-2c.2 handoff §2); pure core merged (PR #553); the create-path wiring + Trigger-#1 prompt render merged (PR #556). Handoffs: `V5_Implementation_Layer4_Slice2c2_TerrainFeasibility_2026_06_11_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` (§2 design, §4 wiring plan) + `V5_Implementation_Layer4_Slice2c2_Wiring_2026_06_12_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` (the wiring).

**Ratified model:** deterministic, **pre-synthesis** resolution (not a post-hoc validator); **make a session that works, never flag-and-prescribe**; route across the whole **cluster** (home + nearby). Two axes — **terrain (this slice)** + **craft (deferred)**. Cascade per discipline: EXACT cluster terrain → PROXY terrain (`terrain_gap_rules` @ fidelity ≥ 0.25, e.g. MTB→road ride) → INDOOR machine (treadmill/stair climber/erg/trainer, gated on a cluster locale's equipment) → STRENGTH substitute (the discipline's own mapped exercises via Layer 2C `ResolvedExercise.discipline_ids`, e.g. climbing→pull/grip) → reallocate. All on **existing layer0 data — no padding, no migration.** D-018 Mountaineering = TRN-005/007/012.

## Layer 0 phase 4 — DB→xlsx bulk-review export (2026-06-11, PR #545) — DONE

**Decision B shipped — the ripe half of phase 4.** `etl/layer0/export_xlsx.py` is a read-only DB→xlsx projection (one sheet per `information_schema`-discovered `layer0.*` table, active rows only) that recovers bulk visual review of all reference data *without* re-introducing the workbook as an authoring input — edits still arrive as `etl/migrations/layer0/` SQL. ## pv=65 cold-plan review + Plans/profile quick-wins (2026-06-11, PR #537) — DONE

**The discipline-mix rewrite is empirically validated.** Andy generated a fresh cold AR plan (**pv=65**); it reached `ready` (00:11 → 01:08) and the allocation is **MTB-dominant** — the win-condition the whole X1–X4 + #509 series was chasing. ✅ One open detail: read `/admin/plan/65/diag` to see whether the bike `load_weight.source` is `race_override` (PGE terrain rows carry per-row `discipline_id`+`pct_of_race`) or `bridge` (riding on the corrected bands alone) — `race_override` moots the #342 terrain-tagging work; `bridge` keeps it owed.

**Generation timing note (→ issue [#539](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/539)) — ⚠️ SUPERSEDED 2026-06-11: the mechanism below was disconfirmed by the untruncated pv=65 logs (see the #539 entry in the Filed-as-issues list).** pv=65 took ~57 min wall-clock because the progress tab was closed for most of it — with the tab closed only the cron drives generation, at ~1 effective pass per ~13 min (each pass holds the advance lock ~470s, next reclaims only after the TTL lapses). Reopening the progress screen drove fast back-to-back passes and finished it. No fault — clean `ready`, cone cached pass 1, no stall/errors.

**PR [#537](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/537) (branch `claude/plan-65-generation-handoff-yzcou4`) — four low-risk quick-wins from the review:**
- **#4** strength sessions were labeled with their associated sport (`discipline_name`) → now **"Strength · <sport>"** (`templates/plan_create/view.html` + `plans/v2/refresh_view.html`). Display-only.
- **#2** coach notes were split (intent under the head, `session_notes` at the card bottom) → grouped both under the head.
- **#8** the §B profile capture cards (supplements/conditions/medications) sat after `.pf-form`, outside its flex gap → `.pf-form ~ .pf-nutrition { margin-top:16px }`.
- **#9** dropped medication-name capture (input+display) — class-only (all Layer 2E screening reads); column + Layer 1 reader untouched. Suite **2281 passed / 30 skipped**, CI green. **NO DDL.**

**Filed as issues (the rest of the pv=65 review — NOT done):**
- ✅ **[#539](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/539)** — **CLOSED `not_planned` + `priority:low` (2026-06-11). Premise disconfirmed.** The untruncated pv=65 logs (issue comment) showed: tab-open is *not* materially faster (the progress poller hits the **same** per-plan advance lock — exactly one pass runs at a time, open or closed), **0 504s / 0 lock-leaks**, and the ~13-min cadence is just inherent per-pass synthesis wall-time. The cron already drives a tab-closed plan to `ready` unattended. **Not a cron bug, not a go-live blocker.** Any future speed-up lives in per-block synthesis cost or the sequential continuity model (prompt/architecture work), not here.
- 🔧 **[#540](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/540)** (high) — sessions prescribed at locales lacking the required terrain (climbing at home). **Slice 2c.2 in flight** — core merged (PR #553), wiring owed; see the dedicated #540 section at the top of this file + the slice-2c.2 handoff.
- ⬜ **[#541](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/541)** — strength too shallow (~4 exercises). Prompt change → stop-and-ask.
- ⬜ **[#542](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/542)** — plan nutrition under-recommends protein (Layer 5A macro formula).
- ⬜ **[#543](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/543)** — health-conditions capture → structured/system-filtered/training-relevant list (#532 follow-up; vocab add).

## Locations privacy surfacing (2026-06-11, PR #535) — DONE, NO migration owed

**PR [#535](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/535) squash-merged to `main`, branch `claude/github-issue-446-lhnk9c`.** Closes **#446** (Track 1 child of #434; Locations epic #427). New locations derived privacy purely from category with no visible indicator and no override — so a residence Mapbox geocoded as `commercial_gym` silently landed shareable ("everything defaults to shared, there's no toggle").

- **UI surfacing, not a model change** (per the issue spec note). `gym_profiles.private` stays source-of-truth; the previously-**dormant** `locale_profiles.sharing_opt_out` column (declared but never read/written) now carries the explicit choice from locale-creation → profile-build. Effective `private = (category ∈ RESIDENTIAL_CATEGORIES) OR sharing_opt_out` via `_resolve_private` / `_category_default_private` in `routes/locales.py`. The opt-out can only **tighten** — residences are never crowd-shareable (the safe default).
- Live private/shared **chip** + **opt-out toggle**: manual `new.html` form (chip updates as category is picked; nonce'd inline JS per the terrain-editor precedent), each Mapbox result card, and the edit `form.html` (own/build mode; residences show a locked "Private" state; `shared_inherit` mode untouched — the shared profile's privacy is its creator's).
- **Crowd-source filtering now reads the explicit flag:** `_find_gym_profile` excludes `private` rows (a peer at the same `mapbox_id` builds their own profile instead of inheriting one its creator marked private; the creator still reaches their own via the `gym_profile_id` link). `delete_locale` cleanup is flag-driven (`created_by_user_id = uid AND COALESCE(private,FALSE)=TRUE`), not re-derived from category — prevents orphaned private profiles from opted-out shareable locales.
- Tests: `tests/test_locales.py` (+10 — `_resolve_private`/`_category_default_private` truth table, `_find_gym_profile` exclusion, build-path opt-out → `private`, flag-driven delete) + render smoke `tests/test_redesign_locales_form_render.py` updated for the new template contract. CI green (Vercel + stubbed unit suite).
- ✅ **NO Neon migration owed** — both `gym_profiles.private` and `locale_profiles.sharing_opt_out` already exist on prod (landed with the Track 1 DDL, item 0 below). Pure code/UI change; live the moment the deploy lands.

   to `_AUTH_EXEMPT_ENDPOINTS`. `…/diag?token=…` now returns JSON (verify after
   the #352 prod deploy). **Note for 504 hard-kills (e.g. plan #48):** a gateway
   504 kills the function before any `except` runs, so `generation_traceback`
   stays null — the diag endpoint shows `generation_status` + `blocks_snapshotted`
   only (localizes how far synthesis got, no traceback). That class is **#350**
   (log-drain backstop) / **#316** (latency). The two original activation
   steps (still relevant for the traceback contents on soft failures):
   surface (Rule #14). Both are optional — the app is deploy-safe without them
   (the traceback persist + the endpoint's traceback read are best-effort):
   - **(a) `python init_db.py` on Neon** — lands the idempotent
     `plan_versions.generation_traceback TEXT` column (container egress to Neon
     is blocked, so this can't run from a web session). Until then, failures
     log the traceback to Vercel only and the diag endpoint returns
     `generation_traceback: null`.

     Claude to fetch `/admin/plan/<id>/diag?token=…` past the app login wall
     (via `web_fetch_vercel_url`). With `DIAG_TOKEN` unset, only the admin
     session can read it (no token bypass). The secret never lives in the repo.
   - Hard-kill backstop (log drain, for 504/OOM before the except runs) is the
     deferred completeness layer — **#350**.

   `plan_versions.advance_lock_until TIMESTAMPTZ` is present on Neon — Andy's run reported the
   column **already existed** (init_db.py applied it on the #419 deploy boot; idempotent no-op).
   The new claim/release SQL is live. Replaces the leak-prone session `pg_advisory_lock` that
   starved pv=56 after a SIGKILL skipped its `finally`.
   - ✅ **6.1 DONE — `PLAN_GEN_FUNCTION_CAP_S=300` set + prod redeployed.** Resulting config:
     `_INVOCATION_BUDGET_S = max(300−330, 30) = 30s` (a pass banks ~1 block ≈169s then returns
     before the ~300s gateway, releasing the lock cleanly); `_ADVANCE_LOCK_TTL_S =
     min(30+280, 840) = 310s` (above one block, well under the 900s stall). **Why:** pv=56's
     block-0 inspect (`latency_ms=168657`, 0 retries, `cap_hit=False`) + the cron log proved the
     budget was mis-sized vs the **real ~300s gateway** — with `=800` the budget was
     `800−330=470s > 300s`, so a pass started block N+1 (≈338s) and got gateway-killed
     mid-flight (what triggered the pv=56 lock leak). Confirms the CLAUDE.md "re-validate the
     800s-cap triage" note — the effective ceiling is the gateway, not 800s.
7. ✅ **DONE (PR #421, 2026-06-05) — #335 strength programming Slices 1 & 2.** The **pv=57**
   cold plan stalled at `Peak:w1`; the logs root-caused it to this exact gap — the per-phase
   prompt rendered only `effective_pool size=N` (a count), never the resolved exercise list →
   the synthesizer **invented `exercise_id`s** → Rule 6a rejected them as `equipment_unavailable`
   (even for gear Andy owns) → the under-specified task drove a **395s empty-output thinking
   attempt** → the 800s timeout. **Slice 1:** `layer4/per_phase.py:_format_strength_exercise_pool`
   renders `=== Strength exercise pool ===` + the `# Strength programming` system prompt (pick
   real ids, never invent; per-phase dose 2/2/1/1; RM/RPE). **`movement_patterns` threaded**
   through 2C (`layer0.exercises.movement_patterns` → query → `ResolvedExercise`) → pattern
   ranking + **data-driven core/accessory** (core = Critical/High priority + compound pattern).

8. **pv=57 carry-forward (non-blocking; from the pulled diag logs, 2026-06-05).**
   - **⚠ CORRECTION to item 6.1's "real ~300s gateway":** that is **WRONG**. The kill is the
     **800s `FUNCTION_INVOCATION_TIMEOUT`** (request `bd6z7-…`, `Duration: 800047ms`), not a
     300s gateway. The cone is a **clean HIT** on reclaim (`ibundle` stable), not re-computing.

     and safe. The earlier "don't raise it" caution was under the now-disproven 300s-gateway
     hypothesis. **Not required** for a successful run.

     now on Layer 2B. Worth a determinism fix (day-anchor / pin the drifting field).
   - **Advance-lock TTL (310s) < real max function duration (800s):** a long pass outlives its
     own lock → a concurrent pass can reclaim mid-flight (duplicate Anthropic spend on a stuck
     block). Align the TTL to the real ceiling, or cap pass wall-clock < TTL.

   plan (pv=58); it stalled at `Build:w2`. Untruncated logs root-caused **two engines**: **(A)** the

- 1 **D-77 poller 500 regression — `'generating'`-mapping + client give-up cap fix (2026-05-29, PR #312).** PR #311 added two `{"status": "generating", ...}` returns to `_advance_plan_generation` (concurrency guard → `advance_in_progress_elsewhere`; per-invocation budget → `budget_partial_progress`) but the poller route `generate_plan` was never taught to handle them — it fell through to `jsonify({"status": "failed", "error": outcome['error']})`, KeyError-ing on the missing key → **HTTP 500 on every intermediate poll**. The budget makes `budget_partial_progress` the *normal* path for any plan needing >1 pass, so essentially every real multi-block plan 500'd to the client's give-up copy ("This is taking longer than expected. Please try again.") even though the cone was healthy and caching blocks. Fix: (1) `generate_plan` maps `'generating'` → `{"status":"generating"}` (keep-polling); (2) `templates/plan_create/progress.html` swaps the *total*-poll cap (`MAX_ATTEMPTS=20` — far too few now each pass caches ~1 week-block) for a *consecutive-transport-failure* cap (a clean response resets it); the server-side `_STALL_WALLCLOCK_S=900`s backstop stays the real terminal guard. 2 code/template files + `tests/test_routes_plan_create.py` (+5 `TestGeneratePlanRoute`); 50 passed in-file, 160 combined. No migration. **This is a prerequisite for owed-deploy #1 (the convergence re-run) — see that entry.** (Walk, deployed + `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`: 1: create a fresh PGE 2026 plan; the progress screen runs for many minutes past the old ~20-poll wall, elapsed counter climbing, and opens the plan on `ready` — no premature "taking longer than expected". 2: mid-flight, `POST /plans/v2/<id>/generate` returns `200 {"status":"generating"}` in devtools→Network, not 500. 3: a genuinely stuck unit still fails loudly via the 900s server backstop → the poller shows the stored failure message, not the generic give-up copy.)

- ✅ **Plan-gen non-convergence — ROOT CAUSE FIXED 2026-05-27 (branch `claude/plan-gen-timeout-logs-caH8Q`).** The instrumented re-run (`plan_version_id=27`) pinned the stall to TWO independent bugs, both now fixed. **(1) Non-deterministic cache keys (the primary bug):** `Layer1Payload.as_of` + `Layer2APayload.rationale_metadata.generated_at` carried a full-precision `datetime.utcnow()` hashed into `layer1_hash`/`layer2a_hash`, which fold into EVERY Layer 4 cache key — so 3A + 3B re-ran cold on every resumable pass (live-run `Layer3A/3BEvidenceBasisWarning` in 17/17 prod passes, ~150s/pass) and any synthesized block was orphaned next pass → D-77 monotonic convergence was structurally impossible (this is why decomposition never helped, and it **overturns the "warm 3A/3B cone" claim in the superseded note below** — the cone NEVER cached across passes; the predecessor had no per-layer cache instrumentation). Fixed by day-anchoring both timestamps (neither is consumed — pure provenance; matches the 3A `as_of` day-granular semantics). **(2) Synthesizer output starvation:** `attempt 1/3 llm call 142528ms (out=9000)` then `tool_args keys=[]` — under thinking the ceiling is `max_tokens(4000)+budget(5000)=9000`, the model spent it all thinking and emitted a contentless tool call → no block cached. Fixed in `invoke_tool_call`: an empty tool call now fires the existing forced-tool retry (thinking off → full output budget, can't decline). Plus a structural **per-block budget** (`_PER_BLOCK_BUDGET_MS=120_000`) in `synthesize_phase`: best-effort accept (caches → progress) or fast terminal (`synthesis_budget_exhausted`), never 504-loops. 4 code files + 13 tests; `Layer4_Spec §11.5` updated. Suite 1793/16 (+13). **No migration. ⚠ Owed (Andy's hands): redeploy (merge) + re-run the PGE plan — expect CONVERGENCE now.** Watch the Vercel log: `synthesize_phase: <phase>:w<n> done —` should fire (it never has), and 3A/3B should NOT re-run every pass. Residual watch-item: if a forced-tool retry truncates a dense ~14-session week against `max_tokens=4000`, bump block-mode `max_tokens` (the budget guard keeps it failing fast, not looping, meanwhile). **✅ WATCH-ITEM FIRED + FIXED 2026-05-27 (branch `claude/plan-gen-schema-violation-tpu23`):** the post-fix re-run no longer 504-looped — it surfaced exactly this bounded `schema_violation`. The per-block budget guard + empty-tool escalation stopped the loop, but the forced-tool retry (thinking off → `max_tokens` IS the whole output budget) truncated a dense week's `sessions` against the 4000 default → empty/partial tool args → `schema_violation`. Fix: block mode (`week_range` set) now sizes the output budget to the unit's session ceiling — `effective_max_tokens = max(max_tokens, max_sessions_this_unit×_BLOCK_OUTPUT_TOKENS_PER_SESSION(600) + _BLOCK_OUTPUT_TOKENS_OVERHEAD(800))` = 9200 for a 1-week block (`layer4/per_phase.py`); whole-phase seam-resynth intentionally unscaled (that's the Slice-3 stitcher's job, not a token bump). 1 code file + 2 tests (`TestBlockOutputBudget`); `Layer4_Spec §11.5` updated. D-77 Slice 1 shrank the cache UNIT (phase→week) but never bounded a block's synthesis COST.** The backstop is healthy; the unit still doesn't fit. Stale `failed` rows stay terminal — start a fresh plan.) **✅ REAL ROOT CAUSE FOUND IN THE PROD LOGS + FIXED 2026-05-27 (branch `claude/review-run-logs-A4JVs`; PR #199 merged `9012430` + PR #200).** This session finally pulled the Vercel runtime logs (every prior session diagnosed code-only). The two failed `plan_version_id=29` runs 504-looped with `max_tokens=9200` live + `schema_violation` GONE but `accepted=True` never firing — i.e. NO block ever converged. **Bug A (the convergence root cause, PR #199):** a SECOND instance of the c4f9160 cache-key non-determinism bug, which that fix missed — `Layer2EPayload.computed_at` (`layer2e/builder.py:1156`) was stamped full-microsecond `datetime.now()`; the cone rebuilds every resumable pass and `computed_at` folds into `layer2e_hash` → `plan_create_key` → EVERY `compute_block_cache_key`, so each pass minted different block keys → every synthesized block orphaned → re-synthesized from scratch each pass → 504-loop re-burning the full extended-thinking synthesis each minute (the ~$50). 2E runs AFTER 3B, so it poisons Layer 4 keys but not 3A/3B — which is why 3A/3B cached fine and only Layer 4 looped, and why the earlier "warm 3A/3B" reads were consistent with a still-broken Layer 4. It also silently defeated the stall backstop (orphan rows kept `_count_cached_blocks` climbing → never plateaued → never tripped). Fix: day-anchor `computed_at` to the cone's logical `today`. Diagnostics added so the next incident is one-read: `cached_wrappers.py` logs `call_cache_key` + each component layer-hash per pass (drift names the guilty layer); `cache.py` logs per-block cache HIT/MISS. **Bug B (PR #200):** after PR #199 deployed, new plans `pv=30..33` failed IMMEDIATELY (`_advance_plan_generation: D-77 stall backstop tripped` on the first pass — impossible for a 900s gate on a brand-new plan). Cause: `_generation_stalled` measured `NOW() - MAX(block.created_at)` scoped to the USER, and `pv=29`'s orphaned rows (>1h old) anchored the window in the past → false-trip on every new plan (bites any user with a prior failed plan). Fix: bound `_generation_stalled` + `_count_cached_blocks` to `created_at >= pv.created_at` (this plan's own progress only). No `Layer 5`/downstream LLM work exists (confirmed: after Layer 4 it's a deterministic persist + `ready` flip), so convergence won't expose a second money-loop. Suite 1796/16. No migration. **⚠ Owed (Andy's hands): merge PR #200 + redeploy, then create ONE fresh plan** — should get past the gate (Bug B) AND converge (Bug A). Coherence (design §14 — do independently-generated weeks blend?) still to verify once a plan reaches `ready`.

- ⚠ **D-77 convergence — the prod re-run found a 3RD cache-key drift (`last_sync`); fixed; re-confirm owed (2026-05-28).** Two fixes landed after #199/#200 (above): the **volume-band pct→hours unit fix (#293)** — the per-discipline `phase_load` bands are percentages but `validator._rule_volume_band` + the synth prompt treated them as hours, firing `volume_band_below` on every discipline + driving an implied ~80h/week over-dense target (the token blowout was downstream of this, not the disease); fixed via shared `validator.phase_volume_bands_hours` + `weekly_capacity_hours` + surfacing `Layer2APayload.weekly_total_hours_by_phase` (previously 2E-only), wired into all 4 volume-rule entry points (suite 1799/16, no migration) — and the **cone cache-key determinism audit (#202)** — swept all cone wall-clock + `uuid`/`date.today` reads. the 2 reads it examined are day-granular — **BUT the audit's "no third money-loop" conclusion was WRONG** (it never scrutinized `last_sync`, an output field, and its guard test used fixed DB rows). **The PGE re-run (`pv=35`) exposed the 3rd drift:** it 504-looped ~6 min then `synthesis_budget_exhausted`; the `synthesize_phase` logs showed `call_cache_key` differing across passes ONLY in `l3a`+`l3b` (l1/l2a–l2e identical) → 3A/3B re-ran every pass → every block orphaned. Root: `ProviderStatus.last_sync` (raw `MAX(webhook_events.received_at)`, `layer4/context.py:952`) rides in the `Layer3AIntegrationBundle` whose hash folds into the 3A cache key; a provider check-in (Andy's COROS/RWGPS) mid-generation drifts it sub-day → 3A miss → temp=1 re-run → l3a drifts → cascades to l3b (3B keys on `layer3a_hash`). The c4f9160/#199 pattern in the one field the audit missed. **Fixed (PR #294):** day-anchor `last_sync` in `q_layer3A_connected_providers` + HIT/MISS + `integration_bundle_hash` diagnostics (3A/3B cached wrappers) + guard test `test_last_sync_is_day_anchored`; suite 1802/16, no migration. **⚠ Owed (Andy's hands): redeploy + ONE fresh PGE plan** — expect `llm_layer3a_athlete_state: … HIT … ibundle=<X>` IDENTICAL across passes, per-block `HIT`, blocks `cap_hit`-cache, plan reaches `ready`; **if `ibundle` STILL drifts**, the diagnostic names the remaining field (likely genuinely-new workout data mid-generation — separate, harder). **Still open (NOT convergence blockers):** (B) `volume_band_below` STILL fires after #293 (best-effort-accepted so non-blocking; likely D-015 Navigation getting a spurious hours-band + primary under-prescribed — needs a modeling decision before touching band logic); (C) ~150s/block latency (`out`≈10k tokens; lever = block thinking-budget/size); (D) `unknown discipline_category` D-015/D-008 + `sport_locale_incompatible_D-008_home` data hygiene. **Optional Trigger-#3 follow-on:** source Layer 2D's date from the cone `as_of` (`q_layer2d_injury_risk_profile_payload`) — eliminates the lone cross-midnight re-key (handoff §6 / D3).
